</p>

***verlaten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlaten.html>verlaten</a> (786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fralētaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlaten.html>verlaten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to leave</li>
<li>to abandon</li>
<li>to desert</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlaten.html>verlaten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlaten.html>verlaten</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verliefdheid.html>verliefdheid</a> (15005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verliefd.html>verliefd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness, -hood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***verliezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verliezen.html>verliezen</a> (812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verliesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*firliosan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fraleusaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verlieren</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λύω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loose, untie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">solvō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dissolve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forlorn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to lose <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">possession</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to lose (a game), to be defeated</li></ol>

***verlopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a> (4794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verlôpen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to progress</li>
<li>to expire, to become invalid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colors</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">clocks</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go fast/slow, to go out of pace
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>Klokken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standaard.html>standaard</a> computersystemen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verlopen.html>verlopen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:seconden.html>seconden</a> per 6 <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> 7 <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a>.</i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://74.125.153.132/search?q=cache:2-Fc-LIVefkJ:handle.dtic.mil/100.2/ADA311584+verlopen+definitionamp;cd=20amp;hl=zh-TWamp;ct=clnkamp;gl=tw">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>Standard computer system clocks can be up to two <a href = vnd.unilang:seconds.html>seconds</a> off per six to seven minutes.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lossen.html>lossen</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlossen.html>verlossen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To free (of something).</li>
<li>To redeem.</li>
<li>To attend the birth of an infant and provide postpartum care to the mother and her infant.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermaken.html>vermaken</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermaken.html>vermaken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to entertain, to amuse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to amuse oneself</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to renovate, to restore</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to adjust, to alter</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermicelli.html>vermicelli</a></i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">vermicello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little worm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">verme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermis.html>vermis</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">-cello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermicelli.html>vermicelli</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">vermicellis</b>)

***verminken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verminken.html>verminken</a> (19741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verminken.html>verminken</a></i>, a dialectal variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vermerken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to injure permanently</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ver-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">manc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a limping or lame person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (cf. Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mank.html>mank</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mancus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">maimed or defective</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*man-ko-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">maimed in the hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*man-</i>
</p>
